		trade_efficiency = 0.1
		republican_tradition = 0.5
	}
	bonus = {
		naval_morale = 0.15
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = RAG
		NOT = { has_country_flag = hie_use_vanilla_ideas }
	}
	free = yes
	hie_rag_saint_blaise = {
		papal_influence = 1
		yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.003
		tolerance_heretic = 1
	}
	hie_rag_liber_statutorum_civitatis_ragusii = {
		all_estate_loyalty_equilibrium = 0.10
		reform_progress_growth = 0.10
	}
	hie_rag_slavic_latin_union = {
		development_cost = -0.10
	}
	hie_rag_republic_ancona = {
		global_ship_trade_power = 0.15
	}
	hie_rag_abolition_slavery = {
		global_unrest = -2
		effect = {
			custom_tooltip = HIE_RAG_ABOLITION_SLAVERY_TT
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { trade_goods = slaves }
					change_trade_goods = random
					remove_building = tradecompany
					if = {
						limit = { has_province_modifier = slave_entrepot }
						remove_province_modifier = slave_entrepot
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	hie_rag_doors_blakans_orient = {
		global_trade_goods_size_modifier = 0.10
	}
	hie_rag_venetian_rivalry = {
		naval_forcelimit_modifier = 0.15
	}
}

						limit = { region = iberia_region }
